< review>
My wife and I were looking for a nice place for an intimate dinner and thought this restaurant looked good. We were a bit under-dressed, but we're greeted warmly and seated promptly.

The service was great - friendly but not overly familiar, prompt and attentive. The food was excellent! We shared the octopus appetizer on the recommendation of our server, and it was superb. My wife had the Hawaiian prawn and potato soup, and it was excellent. She thought her beet salad was only okay, but my turkey sausage pizza was very good.

All in all, we thought the food was excellent, and we would definitely eat there again if we were looking for something special. The only negative I can think of is that the wine list is pretty expensive.</review>

< Review>
The experience working with Lupita's Auto Sales was a complete nightmare.
We live out of state but the drive isn't too far and my father-in-law really liked a vehicle they had at their Modesto location, so we drove to attempt to purchase it.
After taking a look at a few different vehicles a decision was made on one he really liked, there were a few things that needed some work and they offered to fix it or give us a credit for it. We chose to have it fixed, drove back the following weekend to pick-up the vehicle.
After filling out all the paper work needed, we were ready to hit the road!
14 miles into the drive the check-engine light comes on.
We called the office and the "manager" says "no more excuses" whatever that means. We got back to the dealership & were told we could leave the vehicle or getting it repaired in our home state & they would reimburse us.
We decided to take the chance, it drove fine.
Arrived at our destination, safe & sound.

Then came the nightmare of having the vehicle registered.
They insisted on registering it, in the state of California, even though our home state was Nevada.
I legally CANNOT have a vehicle registered in California if I reside in Nevada.
We were told this was being taken care of & we would have a response in no time.
Eventually called a different person who, tells me she knew nothing of our situation & states he would take care of it.
Finally 4 weeks later, after getting passed on to multiple people we received the document we needed to register the vehicle.

Perhaps its that we purchased out of state, but this isn't a place I'd ever recommend.</Review>

<UserId.>106349009591344451905< /UserId.>< user_name>
Josh Hult< /user_name>
<Time>1580933633082<//Time><Rating>5<//Rating>< Text>
I am nearing the end of 12 weeks of physical therapy related to a shoulder injury I sustained at work. First off, I want to state that they make dealing with work comp insurance a breeze. The people that deal with such subjects, behind the scenes, are knowledgeable and do their job well.

My experience with the physical therapy portion has been a great experience also.The staff is professional, courteous, friendly, knowledgeable and compassionate. I believe they do indeed care about the wellbeing of their patients and truly listen to any concerns they may have. Danny and Julia are who I have personally dealt with but in short conversations with other staff, I believe these attributes must be company policy!

The routine they have me doing is challenging but I do see progress. I am asked regularly about my progress (or lack of) and if certain excercises are becoming too easy. They tailor the routine as necessary to provide the best outcome.

I have read all of their reviews and do not agree with the negative ones at all, especially about being left sitting alone. Let me explain. In the beginning they spent any amount of time necessary to help me learn the excercises.  Now I show up and do my excercises as I have been instructed. If you do that, they will keep a distant watch over you and correct anything you are doing incorrectly and remind you if you forget one. I actually appreciate not being hovered over quite a lot! I am an adult and am very capable of continuing my daily routine with minimal staff intervention. It actually enables me to keep busy and finish in a timely manner. From what I have seen the pool is monitored constantly. They deserve a higher rating than they have. A disgruntled patient has obviously affected that...unfortunate!

One part of my own routine is that Danny helps stretch and massages parts of my shoulder. He is great! He is thorough yet gentle at the same time. He pushes me to my limits but never goes beyond them. I also like that it is a personal yet professional experience. I am always greeted by my first name and the conversation can be very interesting. He is a very likeable guy!

The facility is clean and well organized. They wipe down each table after every use. It is in a convenient location with easy access. They do have a pool for aqua therapy but my injury doesn't require me to use it so I can't comment on it. They also offer laser treatments to help with pain (ask them for more info) and have started offering CBD products. I finally agreed to have my first laser treatment today and will update this review after a couple days.

All that being said, I would definitely recommend this place to anyone looking for a great physical therapist. I have been to other places for the same injury and this place beats them all hands down.< /Text>

< text>
Ok... let's be honest, it's hard to find a good plate of Chilaquiles in the high desert to remind you of the home cooking you had growing up..ive had my fair share of some rather bad interpretations of chilaquiles, from soggy oily tortillas to hard tortillas chips with some sort of a mysterious red sauce. I'm gonna skip the whole essay step by step review to just say .... very good home made chilaquiles with an over easy egg and I added the carne Asada on top(my way of eating them) and the reason I gave 5 stars is because they use Cotija cheese on this plate.
